GT 1 GT 2 GT 3 GT 4

  • Check the date of last replacement, both filters elements to be renewed six monthly.

PART III – SEA PHASE

SECTION - A

TRIAL SCHEDULE

Duration for Trials: {{DelhiSix.Duration_Trials}}
Evolution No. Engine Mode Evolution Duration (minutes) Trial Team Check and Record Action
1 As required by SS on all four engines. Start engines and leave harbour.(2 GT/ shaft) As deemed necessary Record idling parameters.
2 Adjust engine regime to 8 kgf/cm² of HPC outlet air pressure. Check balance chamber pressure of all four GTs. 30 min Adjust balance chamber pressure of GTs as per service log. Record all parameters.
3 1 GT/shaft (GT 2 & 3) Continuous Astern (90 SRPM) Disengage GTs 1 & 4 and stop. Rev up GTs 2 & 3 to trial regime. Check balance chamber pressure 30 min Adjust balance chamber pressure of GTs as per service log. Record all parameters.
4 1 GT/shaft ( GT 2 & 3) * 7400 HPC RPM Rev up GTs 2 & 3 to trial regime. 90 min Commence trials after 15 minutes of stabilization. Record all parameters and vibration readings. Run down time of GT 2 & 3.
5 1 GT/shaft (GTs 1 & 4) Continuous Astern (90 SRPM) Start GT 1 & 4 and engage. Disengage GT 2 & 3 and stop. Rev up GTs 1 & 4 to trial regime. Check balance chamber pressure. 30 min Adjust balance chamber pressure of GTs as per service log. Record all parameters.
6 1 GT/shaft ( GT 1 & 4) *7400 HPC RPM Rev up GTs 1 & 4 to trial regime. 90 min Commence trial after 15 minutes of stabilization. Record all parameters and vibration readings. Run down time of GT 1 & 4.
7 2 GT/Shaft 1.0N power of all four GTs in ahead mode Start and engage GT 2 & 3. Rev up GTs to trial regime. 30 min Record parameters after settle down for 10 min.
8 2 GT/Shaft Full astern trials Rev up GTs to trial regime. 15 min Record parameters after settle down for 10 min.

INSTRUCTIONS TO SS: -

1. The following updated documents should be made available before commencement of trials:-

  • Service log of all equipment of GTA .
  • EMAP relevant to equipment and system
  • Record of all adjustments made to elements of engines, RGs and controls.
  • Ships displacement and drafts. State of POLs onboard

2.During vibration signature recording the following precaution need to be undertaken:-

  • Steady course and regime should be maintained.
  • Wheel over 5° to be avoided.
  • Gun trial/helo operation/maneuvering not to be undertaken

3.Engine Room overhead and below platform to be fully illuminated.

4. Temporary lighting arrangements and torches to be provided for inspection inside the engine casing.

5. During trials ensure following:-

  • Ship to remain at even keel without list
  • Steady course to be maintained.
  • Wheel over 5° not permitted.
  • Gun trials/helo operation/maneuvering not permitted.
  • Log ships speed during each recording.
  • Maintain record of equipment running in the E/R and adjacent compartment during recording.
  • Intimate deviations to trial team.

6. Record of lub oil replacement for all four GTsc
